99536	0	0	0	0	CONF	0	0	0	0	0	0	0	0	120	0	true	0	0	0	0	0	0	0	1198	0	4800	0	0	2685	0	0	0	0	0	0	0	0	0									Transfer of chargeoffs from pushdown accounting to reserve for loans related to preacquisition		One Bank of Tennessee (via BPC Corporation, holding company) purchased Citizens First Bank in January 2019. CFB merged with and into OBT in October 2019. The acquisition resulted in a push down accounting adjustment. The push down accounting is analyzed at the end of the 4th quarter annually and adjusted based upon the outstanding balances of the original loans acquired at acquisition date. The adjustment to report RI-B.II reflects a transfer from push down accounting reserves to actual reserves for charge-offs related to the acquisition of CFB and a prorated reduction of the push down accounting balance resulting from paid out loans. The process was reviewed and approved by FDIC Examiners February 2021.

Refer to line 7 below for an explanation of the transaction.				The Company has declared a non-cash dividend of its Private Asset Management (PAM) business to its parent, Teachers Insurance and Annuity Association of America (TIAA), under 12 CFR 5.66 (TIAA Trust Application). TIAA will in turn contribute the PAM business as a non-cash contribution to an advisory affiliate. The OCC by a letter dated October 7, 2025, approved the TIAA Trust Application. The declared non-cash dividend resulted in the recognition of an intangible asset, a corresponding gain, and a dividend liability of $42.4 million, as well as a deferred tax liability of $7.4 million. The net assets of PAM were transferred on January 1, 2026 to TIAA.
